[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: OS Command           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Injection` exception. The sanitizer `OsCommandInjection` flagged a dangerous use of [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ProcessBuilder.start` when invoking external shell commands.                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Type: OS Command Injection – executing operating-system commands    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         with untrusted input can lead to arbitrary code execution.                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m           • `org.apache.tika.cli.TikaCLI` → `TikaAppUnpackerFuzzer`                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m           • The sanitizer hook is triggered during the Tika CLI unpack operation.           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         sanitization.                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         indicating unanticipated input shapes can reach the vulnerable code path.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code Areas for Investigation:                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The `OsCommandInjection` sanitizer logic to understand the exact hook           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m           • `org.apache.tika.utils.ProcessUtils.execute` – how command strings are          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         constructed and passed to `ProcessBuilder`.                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `ShellCodeDetector.detect` method copies an uploaded shell script [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpb, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This runs the script with no arguments under the current user’s privileges, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing arbitrary code execution if the script contains malicious commands.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Jazzer sanitizer hook flags any `ProcessBuilder.start` invocation where [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe command string is derived from untrusted input, giving rise to [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: OS Command Injection`.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Desired Behavior  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still want to detect “no-arg” shell scripts—that is, those that parse [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly without executing any commands—but we must avoid actually running the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscript.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The POSIX shell supports a syntax-only check mode [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`sh -n script.sh`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparses the script for syntax errors without executing its commands. An exit code of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m indicates syntactically valid shell script.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Scope and Constraints  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only `ShellCodeDetector.detect` is modified.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to the fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUnpackerFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or other [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCLI/utility classes.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We continue to support the same tests and CLI behavior; a script detected as [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“no-arg” still sets metadata `sh:[0m[33mno_args[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m` and returns `application/x-sh`.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch avoids external dependency changes and does not widen exception [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcatch scopes.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Proposed Changes in ShellCodeDetector.detect  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Replace the direct invocation of the copied script with a syntax-only [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvocation via the platform shell:  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Before:  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After:  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          List<String> cmd = [0m[1;35mArrays.asList[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"sh"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"-n"[0m[39m, [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtmpFile.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmd[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Keep `[0m[1;35mpb.directory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` so the shell resolves `script.sh` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the temp directory.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Guard against unsupported platforms [0m[1;39m([0m[39moptional but recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If running on Windows [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`SystemUtils.IS_OS_WINDOWS`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, skip any execution [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentirely [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto avoid missing `sh`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and assume the file is a shell script:  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSystemUtils.IS_OS_WINDOWS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Cannot safely perform syntax-only check on Windows; assume shell[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscript  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return SHELL_SCRIPT;  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Retain existing filename sanitization and temp‐directory cleanup logic.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Update inline comments to reflect that we use “sh -n” for a safe syntax check[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than executing the script.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Implementation Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In `ShellCodeDetector.detect`, immediately after `Path tmpFile = [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtmpDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` and `[0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, insert an OS guard:  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSystemUtils.IS_OS_WINDOWS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m On Windows, skip execution; mark as shell script[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return SHELL_SCRIPT;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mpb.directory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      FileProcessResult result = [0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpb, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Use shell syntax-check mode to safely validate the script without [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"sh"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"-n"[0m[39m, [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtmpFile.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mpb.directory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      FileProcessResult result = [0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpb, [0m[1;36m20000[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m100000[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m100000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Leave `[0m[1;35mresult.getExitValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` check intact to set `sh:[0m[33mno_args[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m` when[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe syntax-only check succeeds.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Preserving Existing Logic and Tests  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The method still reads the same metadata, sanitizes the filename, creates a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtemp file, and cleans up the temp directory.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Consumers of `ShellCodeDetector.detect` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding CLI and fuzz harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m only [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobserve that syntactically valid scripts are flagged as “no-arg” and get the same [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmedia type.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change in exit codes or error handling paths outside of preventing [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mside‐effect execution.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigations  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On non-POSIX systems without `sh`, the guard for Windows prevents any attempt [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto execute.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If a user truly needs runtime detection of no-arg scripts on Windows, a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseparate Windows‐specific implementation can be added later [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutside of this [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since the patch only alters the command invocation, other detectors and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsers remain unaffected.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using `sh -n` is a well-known approach to check shell syntax without [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution, eliminating command injection risk.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change is minimal, preserves functional behavior, and removes the critical[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity hole.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, fuzz, or external library modifications are required, complying [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith project guidelines.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach mirrors other codebase usages of syntax-only checks or safe [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterpreter flags in parsers [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee, e.g., hypothetical future `PythonScriptDetector`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musing `python -m py_compile`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The initial issue is a Jazzer-detected security violation                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[1m)[0m in Apache Tika’s `ShellCodeDetector`, where         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         untrusted input is passed directly to an OS command via `ProcessBuilder`, risking   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         OS command injection. A proposed patch modifies `[1;35mShellCodeDetector.detect[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`: it    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         skips shell invocation on Windows by checking `SystemUtils.IS_OS_WINDOWS`, deletes  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the temp directory, returns `SHELL_SCRIPT`, and changes the `ProcessBuilder`        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         invocation to `sh -n [1m<[0m[1;95mfilename[0m[39m>`. After applying the patch, the build fails with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation errors: the `org.apache.commons.lang3` package [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand thus `SystemUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis not on the classpath, so the patch references an unknown symbol.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer fuzz test on `TikaAppUnpackerFuzzer` triggers a [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception for OS command injection.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stack trace highlights that `[0m[1;35mShellCodeDetector.detect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructs a [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ProcessBuilder` with attacker-controlled `fileName`, then calls `[0m[1;35mstart[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This allows execution of arbitrary shell commands embedded in untrusted [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocuments.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerable code resides in [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-core/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/detect/ShellCodeDetector.java`, around the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation of `ProcessBuilder` with `fileName` as the program.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The issue propagates through several layers of Tika’s parsing framework, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39multimately exercised by the Tika CLI in combination with a custom fuzzer harness.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Added an import: `import org.apache.commons.lang3.SystemUtils;`  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Inserted an OS check at line [0m[1;36m98[0m[39m:  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```java[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSystemUtils.IS_OS_WINDOWS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mFileUtils.deleteDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      return SHELL_SCRIPT;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changed the ProcessBuilder instantiation from  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  `ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  to  [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  `ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"sh"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"-n"[0m[39m, [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtmpFile.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Kept the working directory and subsequent `[0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Compilation fails with two errors in `ShellCodeDetector.java`:  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `package org.apache.commons.lang3 does not exist`  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `cannot find symbol: variable SystemUtils`  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This indicates that the patch’s dependency on Apache Commons Lang [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m is not [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresent in `tika-core` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno POM update to include it[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCode Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Dependency configuration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOM[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: verify whether `commons-lang3` can be added, or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse an existing utility for OS detection.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mresult.getExitValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mSHELL_NO_ARGS, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m106[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m107[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m finally [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m108[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mFileUtils.deleteDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m109[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m110[0m[39m:        return SHELL_SCRIPT;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-core/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/utils/SystemUtils.jav[0m[1;92ma:32[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m50[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m:    public static final boolean IS_OS_MAC_OSX = [0m[1;35mgetOSMatchesName[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Mac OS X"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m:    public static final boolean IS_OS_OS2 = [0m[1;35mgetOSMatchesName[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"OS/2"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m:    public static final boolean IS_OS_SOLARIS = [0m[1;35mgetOSMatchesName[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Solaris"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m:    public static final boolean IS_OS_SUN_OS = [0m[1;35mgetOSMatchesName[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"SunOS"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:    public static final boolean IS_OS_UNIX;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:    public static final boolean IS_OS_WINDOWS;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:    private static final String OS_NAME_WINDOWS_PREFIX = [0m[32m"Windows"[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:    public static final boolean IS_OS_VERSION_WSL;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:    private static final String OS_VERSION_WSL = [0m[32m"WSL"[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:    static [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:        IS_OS_UNIX = IS_OS_AIX || IS_OS_HP_UX || IS_OS_IRIX || IS_OS_LINUX || [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIS_OS_MAC_OSX ||[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:                IS_OS_SOLARIS || IS_OS_SUN_OS;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:        IS_OS_WINDOWS = [0m[1;35mgetOSMatchesName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mOS_NAME_WINDOWS_PREFIX[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:        IS_OS_VERSION_WSL = [0m[1;35mgetOSContainsVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[39mOS_VERSION_WSL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:    private static String [0m[1;35mgetSystemProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString property[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause and Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The compilation errors stem from importing [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.lang3.SystemUtils`, which isn’t on Tika’s classpath. Tika [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovides its own `SystemUtils` in `org.apache.tika.utils.SystemUtils`.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The security issue remains: untrusted `fileName` is passed directly to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ProcessBuilder`, allowing OS command injection.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The intended mitigation is to:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Skip shell invocation entirely on Windows [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere `sh` may not exist[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleaning up the temp directory and returning `SHELL_SCRIPT`.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. On non-Windows systems, invoke the shell in “syntax-check-only” mode [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`sh [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-n <script>`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than executing the script.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Update Imports[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Remove the incorrect import:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        import org.apache.commons.lang3.SystemUtils;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Add the Tika-provided `SystemUtils`:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        import org.apache.tika.utils.SystemUtils;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure `FileUtils` remains imported from `org.apache.commons.io.FileUtils`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Modify `[0m[1;35mShellCodeDetector.detect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After copying the uploaded script to a temporary directory and before [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreating the `ProcessBuilder`, insert an OS check:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSystemUtils.IS_OS_WINDOWS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Clean up and bail out on Windows[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mFileUtils.deleteDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return SHELL_SCRIPT;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace the original vulnerable `ProcessBuilder` constructor:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Old [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvulnerable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m – uses untrusted fileName as program[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        with the safe invocation:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m New – syntax-check only, passes fileName only as argument[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"sh"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"-n"[0m[39m, [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtmpFile.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Leave the working-directory setting [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mpb.directory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution via `[0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, and the `finally` block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthat deletes [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tmpDir`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m unchanged for non-Windows platforms.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This ensures that on UNIX-like systems, the shell parser is invoked only [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor syntax checking, with the script name passed as a literal argument [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterpretation of leading “-” or injection of flags[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and on Windows we don’t [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoke any external shell, preventing injection risk entirely.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing file sanitization [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`replaceAll` on `fileName`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and length [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtruncation remain intact.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The working-directory manipulation and the call to [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`—which enforces timeouts and captures exit codes—are [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The detector still returns `SHELL_SCRIPT` in all code paths, preserving the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPI contract.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No New Dependencies or Harness Changes[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We avoid adding `commons-lang3` to the POM by using Tika’s `SystemUtils`.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications are needed to fuzzing harness code or tests.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests and CLI behavior remain unaffected.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On Windows, every file reaching this detector will be identified as a shell [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscript [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`application/x-sh`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, potentially raising false positives. Given that [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWindows shells aren’t available to parse scripts, this is a reasonable fallback. If[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstricter behavior is desired, future enhancements could inspect file extensions or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshebang lines in pure Java without spawning processes.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On UNIX-like systems, invoking `sh -n` may still consume resources for very [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlarge scripts. However, the existing timeouts [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`20s`, `100k` bytes I/O[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m mitigate [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrunaway processes.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tika’s internal `SystemUtils` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-core/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/utils/SystemUtils.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already defines [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IS_OS_WINDOWS`.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar OS-detection patterns exist elsewhere in Tika [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in parsers that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisable certain features on Windows[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSummary of Steps:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. In `tika-core/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/detect/ShellCodeDetector.java`:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove `import org.apache.commons.lang3.SystemUtils;`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add `import org.apache.tika.utils.SystemUtils;`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Insert Windows guard before ProcessBuilder:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSystemUtils.IS_OS_WINDOWS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mFileUtils.deleteDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return SHELL_SCRIPT;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change the `ProcessBuilder` line to:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"sh"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"-n"[0m[39m, [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtmpFile.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Rebuild and verify compilation succeeds.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Run existing unit tests and the jazzer fuzz harness to confirm the OS command [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minjection vulnerability is resolved.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                   [0m[2;36m [0m[34mINFO    [0m Prism Supervisor Routing: TeamStatus.EVALUATE -> TeamStatus.END                      ]8;id=726545;file:///home/user/aixcc/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py\[2m__init__.py[0m]8;;\[2m:[0m]8;id=631725;file:///home/user/aixcc/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py#160\[2m160[0m]8;;\
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mn evals: [1;36m3[0m, patch status: PatchStatus.SOUND[1m)[0m                                        [2m               [0m
